# Collaboration Stamping & Menu Consistency Spec  
**Date:** 2026-02-21  
**Owner:** Staff engineer review pack (YTM/YTD/YTK)  
**Scope:** `js/content_bridge.js`, `js/injector.js`, `js/background.js`, `text.txt`, fixture payloads (`YTM.json`, `YTM-XHR.json`, `YT_MAIN_NEXT.json`, `YT_MAIN_UPNEXT_FEED_WATCHPAGE3.json`) and YTM mobile renderer docs.

## Objective
Define exact collaboration behavior and failure points, then optimize without breaking YTD/YTK parity.  
This spec focuses on:
1. Why `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` cards can miss full collab stamping on mobile watch context.
2. Why uploader-only or ID-only identity still appears.
3. How to keep YTD/YTK behavior stable while fixing YTM.

## What the provided `ytInitialData` snippet is
- `ytInitialData` is a JSON renderer graph for the current page state (watch page payload in this case), emitted by `ytcfg`/YouTube page bootstrap, not an isolated API response.
- `longBylineText.runs[]` is a flattened display string that often concatenates collaborator names (`"GUTSERIEV MEDIA and NYUSHA MUSIC"`), so it should be treated as a hint, not the authoritative roster.
- `showSheetCommand.panelLoadingStrategy.inlineContent.sheetViewModel.content.listViewModel.listItems` is the authoritative structure for collaborator cards in this payload:
  - each `listItemViewModel` contains `title.content` + `leadingAccessory.avatar...` + navigation endpoint (`browseEndpoint.browseId` / `canonicalBaseUrl`)
  - and is parsed by both `extractFromSheetLikeCommand` paths in `content_bridge.js` and `injector.js`.
- For this structure, byline text (including `longBylineText`) is metadata only and should never override or gate the roster extraction result.
- For cards that include this list, this structure is source-of-truth over byline text. Flattened text like `"Shakira and 2 more"` is treated as a hint only.
- For the provided example, this is already the high-confidence collab roster payload (with full channel names + IDs), so parser/validator should prefer it over flattened byline hints.
- The same list can also appear wrapped under neighboring sheet/viewer paths (for example `inlineContent.dialogViewModel.customContent`, `sheetViewModel.content`, `inlineContent.sheetViewModel`, and `content.listItems`), so parser paths must be recursive and tolerant of wrapper shape.
- Quick-cross / quick-block can still work when the menu path is weaker because that flow can use already-stamped collaborator rows from existing DOM/card context while menu enrichment is pending or stale.

### Why these collaborator-ID structures were being missed before
- `js/content_bridge.js` extraction is already resilient for wrapper paths; the remaining miss case came from the matcher gate in `injector.js`.
- For byline forms like `"Shakira and 2 more"`, expected text is often reduced to a single visible token (`Shakira`) while the roster has other collaborators only.
- Previous strict matcher logic required the expected token to match at least one returned collaborator; when it did not, entire 2+ collab rosters were rejected and returned as `null`, leaving placeholders despite valid sheet data.
- Some matched video nodes also contained partial/weak collaborator candidates before the full roster, and the search routine returned early on the first valid roster and stopped scanning nested renderer branches.
- For YTM watch cards with mixed quality candidates, one shallow match can still contain valid but incomplete roster data (e.g. uploader + one collaborator), while the full sheet payload appears deeper in the same node tree. Returning first-match caused deterministic misses for cards like Shakira where the first valid 2-item match was selected.
- Fix now implemented: pass `allowRosterFallbackForCollabMarkup` when hidden-collab markers are detected (`\d+ more`), and allow strong-ID rosters (`>=2` UC IDs) to pass that gate.
- Additional hardening: when only a partial expected marker reaches main-world enrichment, `requestCollaboratorEnrichment` now parses count markers (e.g. `Shakira and 2 more`) into `expectedCollaboratorCount`, sends it as a request hint, and `buildExpectedMatcher` now treats `expectedCollaboratorCount > 2` as roster-fallback enabled even if explicit hint flags are absent.
- Search behavior update: `searchYtInitialDataForCollaborators` now performs ranked candidate selection across all matching videoId nodes, rather than return-on-first-valid. It keeps the highest-quality validator-passing roster (quality + strong UC IDs + matched expectation signals), which prevents shallow partial picks from suppressing deeper full rosters.
  - This was implemented in this pass in `js/injector.js`; fallback to stale DOM only triggers if JSON pass returns no valid list.

## Fix implemented in this pass (no regression intent)
- Normalize and expand expected name hints before matcher checks.
  - Combined text like `"A and B"` and comma/ampersand forms are split into tokenized expectations.
  - This is applied in `js/content_bridge.js` when building `expectedNames` for main-world collaborator requests.
  - This is also applied in `js/injector.js` in `buildExpectedMatcher`, so strict match checks no longer reject valid rosters when hints arrive combined.
- Parse ytm-watch collaborator sheets as first-class input:
  - `content_bridge.js` now resolves sheet-like commands from multiple node wrappers (`showSheetCommand`/`showDialogCommand` + wrapper paths).
  - Recursive scan now looks for `listItems` under multiple nested sheet payload shapes (`panelLoadingStrategy`, `inlineContent`, `sheetViewModel`, `content`, and adjacent wrappers) so `GUTSERIEV MEDIA and NYUSHA MUSIC` rows are hydrated with UC IDs even when short byline text is flattened.
- This change is narrow:
  - It only changes hint matching, not the core acceptance criteria for collaborator extraction.
  - It preserves existing desktop behavior and length/identity quality checks already in place.

## Symptom snapshot
- For video `41ZY18JqI2A`, playlist queue card (`ytm-playlist-panel-video-renderer`) shows expected "All 3+ collaborators" stamping and menu paths.
- On YTM watch-page card (`ytm-video-with-context-renderer`) the collab roster is missing from the card stamp payload; menu and quick-block often surface only uploader identity.
- Same sample has complete collaborator payloads in JSON fixtures:
  - `Shakira and 2 more` byline signal.
  - `showSheetCommand.panelLoadingStrategy.inlineContent.sheetViewModel.content.listViewModel.listItems` with three list items:
    - `shakiraVEVO` (`/channel/UCYLNGLIzMhRTi6ZOLjAPSmw`)
    - `Spotify` (`/channel/UCRMqQWxCWE0VMvtUElm-rEA`)
    - `Beéle` (`/channel/UCYAQgXVSRzUeNo34-RJOWUw`)
- In DOM sample, uploader link is correctly present (`/channel/UCYLNGLIzMhRTi6ZOLjAPSmw`) but full collaborator roster not always stamped.

## Canonical stamping waterfall (current behavior)
1. Check existing stamped attributes on card:
  - `data-filtertube-collaborators`
  - `data-filtertube-expected-collaborators`
  - `data-filtertube-channel-id`, name, handle, custom url
2. Cache lookup:
  - `getValidatedCachedCollaborators(cardId)` in `js/content_bridge.js` and reuse when valid.
3. Card renderer extraction:
  - read renderer/DOM payload from card and fallback endpoints.
4. Byline extraction:
  - parse text runs from byline nodes.
5. Dialog/sheet extraction:
  - parse `showSheetCommand` and/or `showDialogCommand`.
6. Avatar stack extraction:
  - parse `yt-avatar-stack-view-model` or list-item avatar + command context.
7. Fallback parse:
  - parse links, run text patterns, and secondary channel thumbnails.
8. Async main-world enrichment:
  - post `FilterTube_RequestCollaboratorInfo` to `injector`.
  - `injector.js` scans `ytInitialData`, `lastYtInitialData`, `lastYtInitialDataNext`, `lastYtNextResponse` with strict validation.
9. Resolve and apply:
  - `applyResolvedCollaborators` writes collaborators + primary identity fields.

## Waterfall shortcoming notes
- If step 3 extraction fails on ytm-watch cards, later steps can be starved due strictness and short-circuit conditions.
- The ytm-watch path uses different renderer wrappers and menu affordance timing than playlist panel cards.
- ID-only channel capture appears accepted in some fallback paths when name/context is weak.
- Collab identity may be validated out before enrichment returns, causing stale/partial stamps.

## Current flow divergence between playlist and watch-page cards
### Playlist panel (`ytm-playlist-panel-video-renderer`)
- Often gets strong channel context from compact list metadata.
- Stronger chance of byline + menu data on initial render.
- The same collaborator extraction function works with richer compact payload shape.
- Menu fallback path is usually present.

### Watch page (`ytm-video-with-context-renderer`)
- Multiple wrapper layers (`ytm-media-item`, `ytm-bottom-sheet-renderer`, action button nodes).
- Native menu path exists in some states but not always for collab extraction.
- Missing `videoWithContextRenderer` subgraph assumptions can skip collaborator hydration.
- Current output can default to primary uploader only.

## Regression risks to preserve
1. YTD/YTK must not lose explicit channel-name quality guardrails.
2. Never persist video title as channel name.
3. Native YTD/YTK menu behavior and multi-collab menu cap must remain.
4. Avoid regression where stale cache entries with wrong names overwrite good identities.
5. Keep selector breadth bounded to avoid over-blocking unrelated nodes.

## Root cause hypotheses (ranked)
1. High confidence: extraction guardrails around avatar/command nodes are too strict on YTM watch cards.
2. High confidence: `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` often carries collab list in byline `showSheetCommand`, but extraction branch currently treated as low priority after stricter checks.
3. Medium: stale `data-filtertube-last-processed-id` / `mode` state can block re-stamp if asynchronous enrichment returns after first pass.
4. Medium: expected-collaborator count/name validation can reject valid lists if uploader text appears in mixed/Unicode formatting.
5. Medium: menu-only collab source is present while card-only stamp uses a different branch, leaving card and menu desynced.
6. Medium: some fallback paths may store `channelId` as label because `name` could not be confirmed in same pass.
7. Lower: cross-traffic from XHR fixture (`YTM-XHR.json`) suggests payload may exist in continuation chunks not yet reflected in DOM when first card stamp runs.

## Required outcome states
### Must
- Watch-page ytm-card with `Shakira and 2 more` should have full `data-filtertube-collaborators` payload (>=3 entries).
- Uploader name should remain `Shakira`-family string and not degrade to raw UC ID.
- All collab menu rows for 3+ collaborators should be available and actionable.
- Collab row labels must never use generic `Channel` when a stronger identity is available.
  - Use `(handle | mapped handle | customUrl | UC-id)` fallbacks before display text, and replace placeholder-like collaborator names (`Channel`, `All ...`, etc.) as richer identities arrive.
- Playlist and watch variants should both produce consistent channel identity (ID + name).
- Multi-select menu state for two-collab cards should default to `Both Channels`.
- Multi-select menu state for n-collab (n>2) should not enter `0/n` counter mode before user selection.

### Must not
- Do not alter YTD menu behavior for native desktop cards.
- Do not rely on video title to supply channel name.
- Do not block cards purely because one renderer path has weaker metadata.

## Improvement plan (non-regressive)
1. Separate extraction into renderer-path-specific adapters (`ytm-video-with-context`, `ytm-playlist-panel-video`), but keep shared normalized collaborator schema.
2. Add deterministic priority rule:
  - `showSheetCommand.listItemViewModel` should always be source-of-truth when present.
3. For ytm-watch cards, ensure fallback from show-sheet happens even if avatar stack is absent.
4. Keep `channelId` capture but only persist `channelName` when name confidence passes checks; otherwise keep `name:null`.
5. Expand identity stamp refresh policy:
  - allow card re-stamp when collaborators arrive asynchronously and videoId still matches.
6. Add short debug reason tags on skip conditions:
  - `reason=missing-showSheet`, `reason=stale-video-id`, `reason=name-validation-failed`.
7. Add regression guard:
  - if primary identity has UC ID but empty name, attempt same-video `ytInitialData` resolver before render.
8. Create dedicated YTM-watch acceptance matrix:
  - watch related-feed card, upnext, recommendation rail, and playlist queue path.

## Questions (Staff engineer level, 55 total)
1. Why does ytm-watch card still prefer uploader-only stamping when full collab payload exists in fixture JSON?
2. Which extraction branch is actually executed first for `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` right now?
3. Is the branch order identical to playlist-panel cards?
4. In which branch do we map `showSheetCommand` for ytm-watch and what gates exist before that mapping?
5. Do we currently require avatar stack presence before accepting collab lists?
6. Why is uploader ID available without name on some cards?
7. Can uploader ID be intentionally accepted when name confidence is low?
8. What is the exact acceptance criteria for collaborator entry `name` in `content_bridge.js`?
9. Does any ytm-watch path call `invalidateCollaboratorCache` before reattempting extraction?
10. Can a card be re-stamped after asynchronous enrichment if initial pass was partial?
11. Is `shouldStampCardForVideoId` too strict for watch-page dynamic cards?
12. Does `data-filtertube-last-processed-id` ever block valid async updates?
13. What is the exact fallback when `getValidatedCachedCollaborators` fails?
14. What percentage of watch cards show `showSheetCommand` in current fixtures?
15. How often is `shortBylineText` available on watch cards versus compact playlist cards?
16. Is `shortBylineText` parse reused as expected for collab mode classification?
17. How robust is `#attributed-channel-name` fallback for ytm-watch cards?
18. Do we parse both `title` and `subtitle` in list items from showSheet list payloads?
19. Are canonicalBaseUrl and browseId both required or is one enough for identity?
20. Does commandContext browseEndpoint provide better identity than title.commandRuns?
21. Are handles extracted from `subtitle` normalized before dedupe?
22. Why is handle sometimes not shown in menu while ID exists?
23. Are mixed name/ID pairs being rejected in identity merge?
24. Can mismatched handle+id from different collaborators accidentally get merged?
25. Is there a dedupe key conflict between collaborators and primary channel in storage?
26. Are duplicate collaborators merged deterministically before rendering menu rows?
27. What is the exact cap for collaborators in YTM mobile menu flow?
28. Does this cap differ from YTD/YTK collab menu cap?
29. If we return 6 collaborators, does quick-block button label still reflect pluralization?
30. What is the expected behavior if three collaborator channels are all unresolved by name?
31. When unresolved, should card still expose quick-block-all?
32. Should unresolved name fallback display handle text instead of ID?
33. Where is the boundary between strong and weak validation for names?
34. What is the failure mode for channel names containing non-ASCII punctuation or symbols?
35. How are RTL/LTR names handled in name extraction?
36. Should `@handle` be preferred over `channel name` when both conflict?
37. Does the mobile menu branch currently parse `listItemViewModel.title.commandRuns` correctly when `title.content` differs?
38. What is the confidence rule when `browseId` appears but `canonicalBaseUrl` is missing?
39. Can `browseId` for primary uploader be same as one collaborator entry causing overwrite?
40. Do we persist a collaborator list where first entry differs from primary identity intentionally?

43. If primary and collaborator overlap by ID, do we de-duplicate or preserve duplicate-free order?
44. What telemetry exists for miss reasons at every extraction layer?

46. Do we currently stamp `data-filtertube-collaborators` with a stable JSON schema on all paths?
47. Is schema versioned for future compatibility in `channelMap`?
48. Could old cards keep old incomplete values forever due no invalidation on SPA rerender?
49. Is there a `mode` difference (blocklist vs video) that prevents re-stamping in watch context?
50. Can we verify ytm-watch watch page cards by reusing the same extraction schema as mobile home/search cards?
51. Is there any selector path using `shortBylineText.runs[*].navigationEndpoint` for ytm-watch not yet implemented?
52. Are we handling `longBylineText`/`shortBylineText` alternates uniformly across mobile surfaces?
53. Can we validate that watch page card and menu both receive same resolved collaborators in one enrichment cycle?
54. Which async race condition can cause menu rows to be correct while card attributes are stale?
55. What exact acceptance metric defines “collab consistency” across YTM watch card and playlist panel for the same `videoId`?
## Answers and proposed implementation decisions

## Proposed fix plan
1. `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` adapter path in `js/content_bridge.js`.
   - New first-class parse path:
     - `shortBylineText` -> `navigationEndpoint` -> `showSheetCommand`.
     - `showSheetCommand.panelLoadingStrategy.inlineContent.sheetViewModel.content.listViewModel.listItems`.
     - Parse `listItemViewModel.title`, `title.commandRuns`, `rendererContext.commandContext`, `subtitle`.
   - Implemented in this pass: command resolver and recursive list-item walker are active.
   - Do not gate success on avatar stack presence.
2. Make show-sheet list items the highest-confidence source for collab hydration when present.
   - Write `data-filtertube-collaborators` from parsed list first.
   - Write primary fields from best strong first entry.
3. Re-stamp policy update for async enrichment:
   - In `shouldStampCardForVideoId` and `applyResolvedCollaborators`, allow overwrite if same `videoId` and enriched payload has higher collaborator cardinality or better confidence.
4. Prevent ID-only display leakage:
   - In menu/card rendering, prefer name, then handle, never UC-only as user label.
5. Add cache-quality metadata (`source`, `confidence`) in collaborator cache result objects.
   - This controls re-stamp decisions deterministically.
6. Add miss diagnostics:
   - `missing_renderer`, `missing_showSheet`, `missing_listItems`, `no_valid_identity`, `stale_processed_gate`.
   - Emit through existing debug logging path only.
7. Keep YTD/YTK untouched:
   - no behavior changes in desktop/YTK selectors unless this causes parity breakage.
8. Add fixture-backed validation for `41ZY18JqI2A` on:
   - watch page card (`ytm-video-with-context-renderer`)
   - playlist queue card (`ytm-playlist-panel-video-renderer`)
   - any equivalent home/search surface with `Shakira and 2 more`.

## Immediate corrective action (already applied)
- `applyResolvedCollaborators` had an incorrect dual guard that could skip `force: true` updates whenever incoming quality was lower than cached quality.
- Replaced the guard with a deterministic rule:
  - block overwrite when cached quality is higher unless `force` is true
  - only allow `allowSourceCardRewrite` to bypass this block for the explicitly provided `sourceCard`
- This preserves higher-quality cached lists while still allowing async source-card reconciliation for YTM watch cards.

## Validation expectations (no code run required in this phase)
- Watch card should expose `data-filtertube-collaborators` with names matching all three collaborators for the sample case.
- Menu and card should show consistent channel IDs/names for same `videoId`.
- YTD/YTK regression matrix remains unchanged with respect to:
  - no video-title-as-name persistence
  - non-empty menu behavior for multi-collab cards.

## Post: 50-item review (YTM watch-card + playlist parity, 2026-02-21)

### Why this post exists
The new failure class is not missing API data; it is orchestration/normalization mismatch:
- `ytInitialData` includes collaborator list in `showSheetCommand`.
- Watch card menu can still remain in placeholder / resolving while data exists.
- Playlist cards and some watch cards differ in renderer behavior and enrichment timing.

### 50 questions and proposed answers
1. Why does the fallback placeholder remain on Shakira watch-card while collab data exists in initial payload?
   It is most likely blocked by early parse gating and asynchronous overwrite rules that treat the initial result as already “good enough.”
2. Why does Nyusha’s placeholder show resolved rows only after delay while quick block already works?
   The quick block uses a separate payload (card-level quick attributes) while 3-dot menu relies on another enrichment path that can lag.
3. Why do some menu rows show UC IDs instead of names?
   Name confidence checks are failing and fallback logic permits ID to surface as display text.
4. Should IDs ever be rendered to users when names are available in `showSheet`?
   No. IDs are never preferred display labels.
5. Which path should be source of truth for names on YTM?
   `showSheetCommand.listItems` should be the highest priority source when present.
6. Why do playlist cards work but watch cards don’t?
   Watch cards pass through a different renderer envelope and require adapter-specific extraction branches.
7. Is there parity intent between YTD and YTM parsing order?
   Intent is parity in schema and behavior, but not identical DOM selectors.
8. Can we keep behavior parity without identical selectors?
   Yes via shared normalized schema and renderer-specific extractors.
9. Is this a full regression or partial surface regression?
   Partial: same `videoId` can behave differently across watch and queue surfaces.
10. Are these failures deterministic or random?
   Mostly deterministic per surface/DOM timing, with random-like variance due async re-render timing.
11. Does `ytInitialData` for these samples contain collaborators in list form?
   Yes, both Shakira and Nyusha payloads show `listItems`.
12. If list exists, why do menus remain placeholders?
   Extraction is not always applied to menu context in the ytm-watch branch.
13. Is the placeholder string “Fetching collaborators…” expected user-facing state?
   Only transiently and must auto-resolve to names shortly after.
14. Is “All (pending…)” allowed only in desktop?
   No, can appear in mobile fallback as unresolved enrichment state and should resolve quickly.
15. Why does quick block sometimes block all correctly while menu still pending?
   Different execution path and timing, with quick block often using already-enriched collaborator set.
16. Could quick block be using stale cached collaborators while menu is live?
   Yes, if cache refresh criteria are too strict.
17. Does re-stamp logic allow higher-quality async updates?
   Present logic may reject better payload due strict lock/state checks.
18. Should re-stamp allow same `videoId` regardless of previous mode?
   Yes when richer collaborator payload or stronger confidence is available.
19. Do we currently classify collab cards by both byline and collaborators length?
   Inconsistent across paths; consistency is required.
20. How should collab card detection behave for “X and 2 more” text?
   As a hint only, not as final proof.
21. Should parser trust “longBylineText” if short byline is absent?
   Yes, prefer whichever has stronger collaborator structure and command link context.
22. Should avatar-stack presence be mandatory?
   No.
23. Should collaborator capture require `browseId`?
   `browseId` preferred, but fallback to strong name+handle may be accepted with lower confidence.
24. What if two collaborators share the same display name?
   Deduplicate by `browseId` first, fallback to handle canonicalization.
25. Should handle extraction prefer local `title.content` or `subtitle`?
   Use both, with higher trust for explicit `customUrl` / handle forms.
26. What if subtitle contains noisy RTL/LTR markers?
   Strip directional marks before normalization.
27. Are non-ASCII names broken in normalization?
   No, treat as valid and avoid ascii-only assumptions.
28. Should we parse `title.commandRuns` even when `title.content` exists?
   Yes, because command context often carries definitive identity.
29. Should `data-filtertube-collaborators` be overwritten on each enrichment?
   Only when confidence improves or missing keys are filled.
30. Can stale `data-filtertube-last-processed-id` block updates?
   Yes for weakly implemented paths; should allow explicit enrichment override for matching video ID.
31. Should `data-filtertube-last-processed-mode` block cross-surface updates?
   No when source payload proves superior completeness.
32. Do we need a dedicated YTM-watch adapter in content bridge?
   Yes and this is central for long-term consistency.
33. Can we share extractor tests between YTM watch and playlist?
   Share canonicalization and dedupe tests; keep DOM selectors separate.
34. Why does Nyusha show `(resolving…)` even with complete list?
   IDs are extracted but name binding may be delayed/lost before post-normalization.
35. Should unresolved collab rows be interactive?
   They should remain present and non-blocking with clear status.
36. How should disabled rows be surfaced?
   `disabled` only for in-progress state, not terminal failure.
37. Should fallback menu rows include “All Collaborators (resolving…)” for all cases?
   Only while enrichment is pending; remove placeholder once list arrives.
38. Is duplicate quick-block all button behavior a conflict risk?
   Not if rows share deduped IDs and consistent labels.
39. Should quick block label include “All channels” if exactly one uploader + one collab?
   Prefer “All” semantics with count-neutral copy.
40. What is the conflict between blocklist mode and video mode?
   There should be no conflict as both operate over channel IDs.
41. Can three-dot menu and quick block disagree on the set?
   They should never disagree for same `videoId`; if they do, flag mismatch event.
42. Do we emit mismatch telemetry today?
   Minimal; should add structured reasons.
43. What minimum debug signal is enough?
   Reasoned source + stage + outcome code per card.
44. Does YTM mobile need fewer rows than desktop?
   Keep semantic parity; adapt UI width only.
45. Can menu rendering be done from cache without re-reading `ytInitialData`?
   Yes, once cache has source+confidence tags.
46. What cache metadata is needed for rehydration?
   `source`, `count`, `confidence`, `updatedAt`, `incompleteReason`.
47. Should we version collaborator schema?
   Yes, minimally `schemaVersion` in cache payload.
48. Do we need to avoid mutating existing complete YTD cards?
   Yes; guard with `source === ytd-native` stable path.
49. What are acceptance criteria for this fix?
   Watch card + playlist card converge on same `videoId`, collaborator IDs, and display names.
50. What if no collaborator list can be proven for a card?
   Keep explicit “unable to resolve” state and never show raw IDs as labels.

### Proposed patch strategy (post entry)
1. Introduce a YTM watch-card extractor branch in `js/content_bridge.js` that parses `showSheetCommand -> listItems` unconditionally when present.
2. Route that extracted list through shared normalization to produce:
   - `name` (primary),
   - `handle`,
   - `channelId`,
   - confidence tag.
3. Update menu/quick-block render paths to use `name > handle > id`; hide IDs from user-facing labels unless both missing.
4. Relax same-`videoId` lock in re-stamp logic when enriched payload increases:
   - collaborator count,
   - confidence score,
   - field completeness.
5. Keep fallback states (“pending/resolving/fetching”) short-lived and attach explicit timeout/expiry to avoid infinite pending UI.
6. Keep YTD/YTK untouched by feature-flagging this as “YTM-watch adapter + normalized async merge” only.
7. Add structured diagnostics for each card:
   - `missing_sheet`, `missing_listItems`, `menu_render_id`, `menu_render_name`,
   - `merge_skipped_by_cache`, `merge_applied_by_force`.
8. Validate against existing fixture cases:
   - Shakira (`41ZY18JqI2A`) should render all three names in both surfaces,
   - Nyusha payload should render name-backed collaborators and eventually remove “resolving…”.

## Post Entry: 50 staff-level QA + decisions (YTD/YTM collab card consistency)
**Date:** 2026-02-21  
**Context:** `YTM` and `YTD` collab-card behavior, with priority on resolving `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` misses and menu/quick-block parity.

### 1) Why does `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` miss full collab stamping while data exists in fixture payloads?
Because the watch-path branch does not currently treat `showSheetCommand` as a high-priority mandatory source, so it often exits earlier.

### 2) Which extraction branch executes first for watch cards today?
Cache validation is still checked first, then renderer extraction; however watch-specific branch weight is effectively lower than list-card paths.

### 3) Why is branch order not identical across playlist and watch surfaces?
They are routed through different render adapters, so fallback arrays and priority conditions differ.

### 4) Is `showSheetCommand` parsed for watch cards and what guards block it?
Yes, but it can be gated by branch assumptions and dependency on other nodes that are not present in this renderer.

### 5) Does watch path still depend on avatar stack before accepting collaborators?
In practice, yes in several paths; this is too strict and should be removed.

### 6) Why can uploader ID appear without its name?
Name confidence/validation can fail while ID is still captured, and ID gets retained as fallback identity.

### 7) Should ID-only identity be treated as final display data?
No. IDs must remain non-UI display fallback only and trigger resolving state when no valid name exists.

### 8) What is the exact current name acceptance criteria?
Normalization plus confidence checks in the bridge; if checks fail, name is either scrubbed or marked unresolved.

### 9) Is there a watch-card cache invalidation before re-parse?
Not consistently. Reparse gating is conservative; it can block repeated enrichment opportunities.

### 10) Can cards be re-stamped after partial initial pass?
Not reliably; stale `last-processed` checks often prevent re-stamp, especially on async updates.

### 11) Is `shouldStampCardForVideoId` too strict for dynamic watch cards?
Yes when `videoId` extraction is unstable during render cycles.

### 12) Can `data-filtertube-last-processed-id` block valid updates?
Yes, if mode+videoId state does not transition, newer resolved collaborators can be ignored.

### 13) What does `getValidatedCachedCollaborators` do on failure?
It drops invalid cache and falls back to extractor path, then async enrichment.

### 14) How often does `showSheetCommand` appear in current watch fixtures?
Unquantified; needs event counters to avoid guesswork.

### 15) Is `shortBylineText` consistently present on watch cards?
Not consistently; it is one of several weak signals.

### 16) Is byline parsing still part of collab detection?
Yes, but it should not be treated as final authority without higher-confidence sheet/list parsing.

### 17) Is the byline fallback robust enough on watch?
No; it is insufficient in some variants and needs stronger watch-specific handling.

### 18) Do we parse both title and subtitle in list items?
Partially; parse paths vary by adapter and should be normalized.

### 19) Is `browseId` enough for persistence?
Yes, for stable identity. Canonical URL is optional metadata.

### 20) Is command-context generally stronger than title parsing?
Generally yes; it is usually less ambiguous.

### 21) Is handle normalization done before dedupe?
Partially; not guaranteed across all paths.

### 22) Why is handle absent while ID exists in UI?
Because handle-bearing branches may be skipped when watch branch conditions fail.

### 23) Can mismatched handle/id pairs merge incorrectly?
Yes if dedupe keys are not strictly ID-first.

### 24) Can mismatched pairs be accidentally merged later?
Yes, without strict conflict checks and source confidence comparison.

### 25) Can primary channel and collaborators collide in cache keys?
Potentially, unless explicit key namespaces or role tags are used.

### 26) Is duplicate collaborator de-dup deterministic?
Not guaranteed today for all paths; deterministic order + ID-first dedupe is required.

### 27) What collaborator cap is active for YTM mobile?
Practical cap remains 6 (subject to UI width/row rendering).

### 28) Must YTM cap equal YTD/YTK?
Yes, to avoid platform drift and UX inconsistency.

### 29) Does quick-block-all label behavior hold with variable counts?
Only after normalization; edge cases need explicit pluralization handling.

### 30) What if all collaborators are unresolved names?
Keep actionability via identifiers, but keep UI labels in handle/resolving forms, never raw IDs.

### 31) Should quick-block-all remain enabled while unresolved?
Yes if collaborator count is inferred and at least one stable identifier exists.

### 32) Should unresolved fallback use handle over ID?
Yes, handle is preferred over raw ID for display.

### 33) Where is weak-vs-strong name boundary?
At sanitization + confidence heuristics; must be aligned across all surfaces.

### 34) Are Unicode-heavy names currently at risk?
Yes; regexes can over-reject valid non-ASCII names.

### 35) Is RTL/LTR handling addressed?
Not explicitly; parsing should remain script-safe and avoid destructive normalization.

### 36) Should handle override channel name if conflicting?
No; explicit channel names remain higher priority.

### 37) Does watch path parse list title command runs consistently?
Not fully; adapter gap exists.

### 38) Should `browseId` alone pass when canonical URL missing?
Yes, with lowered confidence penalty but acceptable persistence.

### 39) Can primary uploader and collaborator IDs collide?
Possible if extraction is ambiguous; dedupe should preserve first-seen unique IDs.

### 40) Can stored collaborator list intentionally differ from primary identity?
Yes, by source semantics, while ensuring dedupe and ordering rules.

### 41) Is uploader expected to be first in this sample?
Yes, this fixture’s list suggests uploader/primary appears first.

### 42) Quick-block-all should include uploader?
Yes, currently intended behavior is uploader + collaborators after dedupe.

### 43) De-duplicate behavior for overlap?
Use strict ID-first dedupe while preserving first-seen order.

### 44) Is extraction miss telemetry complete?
No. Add structured reason codes per layer.

45) Can we have structured failure logs in debug mode?
Yes, and should be added for watch-card misses.

### 46) Is collaborator schema stable across YTD/YTM outputs?
Mostly stable but should include explicit source/confidence metadata.

### 47) Is cache schema versioned?
Not enough for migration safety; add explicit metadata fields to avoid ambiguity.

### 48) Can old incomplete cards persist forever?
Yes, without re-entry invalidation and enrichment overwrite rules.

### 49) Can mode (`blocklist` vs `video`) block re-stamp?
Potentially; mode gating must allow enrichment upgrades for same `videoId`.

### 50) How do we define collab consistency for this task?
Same `videoId` must result in same collaborator ID set and normalized display in card and menu within one enrichment cycle.

### Post decision (YTD/YTM fixes policy)
1. Scope the immediate fix to `ytm-video-with-context-renderer` and retain current YTD desktop and YTK behavior unless a regression is proven.
2. Enforce source priority: show-sheet list items (when present) outrank avatar/byline-only heuristics.
3. Never render UC IDs in user-facing labels; render `handle`, then `name`, then `resolving`.
4. Add one-way reconciliation for menu/card from a single resolved payload per `videoId`.
5. Allow async overwrite when newly resolved payload has higher cardinality/confidence, even if earlier partial payload exists.
6. Add reason-code telemetry for every collab extraction miss path and missing name-quality path.
7. Add fixture-backed checks for `41ZY18JqI2A` across watch-card and playlist-card surfaces.
- If source has only partial data, card should include debug markers and degrade gracefully instead of ID-only display when name unavailable.
